The default error handler will requeue the event (by its key) for\n    48→// later retried processing. The requeueing is rate limited and can be configured with\n    49→// WithRateLimiter option to Events().\n    50→//\n    51→// The resource is lazy, e.g. it will not start the informer until a call\n    52→// has been made to Events() or Store().\n    53→type Resource[T k8sRuntime.Object] interface {\n    54→\t// Resource can be observed either via Observe() or via Events(). Each event must be marked as handled\n    59→\t// with a call to Done() which marks the key processed. No new events for this key\n    60→\t// will be emitted before Done() is called.\n    61→\t//\n    62→\t// A missing Done() will lead to an eventual panic (via finalizer on Event[T]).\n    63→\t// Panic on this situation is needed as otherwise no new events would be emitted\n    64→\t// and thus this needs to be enforced.\n    65→\t//\n    66→\t// A stream of Upsert events are emitted first to replay the current state of the\n    67→\t// store after which incremental upserts and deletes follow until the underlying\n    68→\t// store is synchronized after which a Sync event is emitted and further incremental\n    69→\t// updates:\n    70→\t//\n    71→\t//\t(start observing), Upsert, Upsert, Upsert, (done replaying store contents), Upsert, Upsert,\n    72→\t//\t  (store synchronized with API server), Sync, Upsert, Delete, Upsert, ...\n    73→\t//\n    74→\t// The emitting of the Sync event does not depend on whether or not Upsert events have\n    75→\t// all been marked Done() without an error. The sync event solely signals that the underlying\n    76→\t// store has synchronized and that Upsert events for objects in a synchronized store have been\n    77→\t// sent to the observer.\n    78→\t//\n    79→\t// When Done() is called with non-nil error the error handler is invoked, which\n    80→\t// can ignore, requeue the event (by key) or close the channel. The default error handler\n    81→\t// will requeue.\n    82→\t//\n    83→\t// If an Upsert is retried and the object has been deleted, a Delete event will be emitted instead.\n    84→\t// Conversely if a Delete event is retried and the object has been recreated with the same key,\n    85→\t// an Upsert will be emitted instead.\n    86→\t//\n    87→\t// If an objects is created and immediately deleted, then a slow observer may not observe this at\n    88→\t// all. In all cases a Delete event is only emitted if the observer has seen an Upsert. The default error handler will requeue the event (by its key) for\n// later retried processing. The sync event solely signals that the underlying\n\t// store has synchronized and that Upsert events for objects in a synchronized store have been\n\t// sent to the observer.\n\t//\n\t// When Done() is called with non-nil error the error handler is invoked, which\n\t// can ignore, requeue the event (by key) or close the channel. The default error handler\n\t// will requeue.\n\t//\n\t// If an Upsert is retried and the object has been deleted, a Delete event will be emitted instead.\n\t// Conversely if a Delete event is retried and the object has been recreated with the same key,\n\t// an Upsert will be emitted instead.\n\t//\n\t// If an objects is created and immediately deleted, then a slow observer may not observe this at\n\t// all. In all cases a Delete event is only emitted if the observer has seen an Upsert. Whether or\n\t// not it had been successfully handled (via Done(nil)) does not affect this property.\n\tEvents(ctx context.Context, opts ...EventsOpt) <-chan Event[T]\n\n\t// Store retrieves the read-only store for the resource. It watches CiliumNetworkPolicy resources\n// and maintains per-namespace counts.\nfunc (pc *PolicyQuotaController) Run(ctx context.Context) error {\n\tcnpEvents := pc.ciliumNetworkPolicies.Events(ctx)\n\n\tfor {\n\t\tselect {\n\t\tcase <-ctx.Done():\n\t\t\treturn ctx.Err()\n\t\tcase event, ok := <-cnpEvents:\n\t\t\tif !ok {\n\t\t\t\treturn nil\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\tvar err error\n\t\t\tswitch event.Kind {\n\t\t\tcase resource.Upsert:\n\t\t\t\terr = pc.onPolicyUpsert(event.Object)\n\t\t\tcase resource.Delete:\n\t\t\t\terr =
